[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA heap-based buffer overflow was detected by AddressSanitizer in the libexif [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibrary when processing EXIF data. The overflow occurs in the function [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_get_slong` within `exif-utils.c`, as it reads one byte past the end of an [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated buffer while parsing Fuji maker-note data. This issue was found by a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibFuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_from_data_fuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m running under interactive fuzzing mode.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The sanitizer log reports a “heap-buffer-overflow” vulnerability. A one-byte read[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moccurs beyond the bounds of a dynamically allocated [0m[1;36m56[0m[39m-byte region.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerable Code Path  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer entry point [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_from_data_fuzzer.cc`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m feeds arbitrary data into `exif_data_new_from_data`.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Inside `exif_data_new_from_data` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min `exif-data.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, data is loaded via [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_data_load_data`.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The load function dispatches to `exif_mnote_data_fuji_load` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif-mnote-data-fuji.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. During parsing of a Fuji-specific metadata tag, `exif_get_long` and its helper[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_get_slong` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min `exif-utils.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are called.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. `exif_get_slong` reads past the end of its input buffer, triggering the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The overflow address [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0x50600000011f[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes beyond the allocated [0m[1;36m56[0m[39m-byte [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap block.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The sanitizer trace pinpoints line [0m[1;36m137[0m[39m in `exif-utils.c` as the exact overflow [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msite.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The Fuji maker-note loader [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif-mnote-data-fuji.c`, line [0m[1;36m175[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m invokes the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfaulty routines without apparent bounds checks for this read.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The issue consistently reproduces under fuzzing with a single test case, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating a deterministic out-of-bounds access.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Investigation Scope  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To fully assess the impact and context of this overflow, examine:  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • exif-utils.c around `exif_get_slong` and `exif_get_long` for boundary [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • fuji maker-note loader in `exif-mnote-data-fuji.c`, especially how tag offsets,[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libFuzzer run of `exif_from_data_fuzzer` against libexif triggered an [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer heap-buffer-overflow in `exif_get_slong` when parsing Fuji [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaker-note data. The overflow arises during a call chain of `exif_get_slong` → [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_get_long` → `exif_mnote_data_fuji_load`. To guard against out-of-bounds [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreads, a patch was proposed in `libexif/fuji/exif-mnote-data-fuji.c` adding a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mCHECKOVERFLOW[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdatao + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, buf_size, [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` before calling `exif_get_long`. Applying [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat patch, however, produced numerous compilation errors [0m[1;39m([0m[39mundeclared identifiers [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlike `buf` and `datao`, malformed control flow, extraneous braces[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m indicating the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch was mis-merged or dropped crucial context.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer log reports a one-byte heap-buffer-overflow at address [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;36m0x50600000011f[0m[39m` during a read in `exif_utils.[0m[1;92mc:137[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_get_slong`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The stack trace shows this occurs inside `exif_mnote_data_fuji_load` when [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreading maker-note data from a buffer of size smaller than expected.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - ASan’s shadow memory and allocated region details confirm the code read one [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbyte past a [0m[1;36m56[0m[39m-byte allocation, leading to the crash.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Key Observations  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The offending code path calls `[0m[1;35mexif_get_long[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + datao + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mEXIF_BYTE_ORDER_INTEL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` without verifying that the buffer has at least [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavailable at that offset.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The variables in scope at the failure point include `buf` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyte pointer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`buf_size` [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize of the buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and `datao` [0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset into `buf`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
